It is a ten-minute walk from the high-speed rail station, but the sun is hot outside. The hotel has a dedicated laundry room, swimming pool, and gym, which is very considerate. The front desk also provides souvenirs for check-in, and there is a book bar in the lobby. If you come to Changsha and want to live here near the high-speed railway station, it is right. There are subway Pingyang Station and Changsha South Station a few hundred meters nearby, which is very convenient. Next time you come to Changsha, you will want to live here.
